I think I would be worried about weekly updates. It's fine to work on updates for long periods of time because then you can thoroughly develop and test update ideas. Longer gaps between updates is far better than rushed updates that are buggy or aren't well thought out. I'm also worried about the health of the devs themselves, I've seen a lot of roblox games with developers that just get burnt out and lose inspiration or interest in developing the game. So, while weekly updates sound cool and all, I don't think its practical, and I don't believe that anyone is really pushing for such a quick update schedule. Y'all can chill with that.

not sure how i feel about the  weekly updates thing. first of all, i would like to congratulate this game on its quality- its truly amazing, which is the reason i started playing in the first place and why i was able to cope with slow updates. Every time a new update was announced , i could expect enjoyable quality that i knew was nice. but with weekly updates, i dont want devs cramping and not getting sleep over releasing a quality update, nor do i want a badly made update. I also really dislike the concept of a new fruit every week. that would make all of the existing fruits feel really not so valuable. other than that, i really like how this whole thing sounds.

What about the revamped fruits that were mentioned on twitter?
I would like to voice my opinion about weekly updates. It was stated that there will be weekly fruits. I feel that this is a bad idea. Fruits have been getting better and better over time and if this same pattern continues, many older fruits will be heavily outclassed. I think that powercreep will be a huge issue in weekly fruits. I would also like to point out that weekly updates can make a game feel daunting for new players due to the addition of high amounts of new content. I know that Blox Fruits has been getting very big recently and I do think the game does deserve this. I have been playing for a pretty amount of time and have seen this game grow. However, I am not sure if this is the proper way for the game to be going. rant concluded  Edit: To address the many points about reworks on old fruit, that does nothing to fix the issue of new fruits powercreeping older ones. It would be insane for old fruits to get reworked just after the addition of a new fruit. I would also like to say that the slow addition of updates made the few updates that did happen gain hype. They made people look forward to an update coming out and whenever it did come out in would re instill all of the attachment to the game that the player base had. I used to play a MMORPG with a similar issue that I am predicting. There was a set amount of things in the game until the game got traction. The developers decided to do weekly updates, each giving better and better equipment. It was fun for a little, however the player eventually got desaturated on it and stopped playing. I do enjoy this game a lot and do not want it to go down the wrong path. Again, I do see your point about older fruits getting reworks, however that is not fixing the issue and instead just delaying it. It is unethical for that to happen for a prolonged amount of time.
